    function insertParam(key, value, search) {
      key = encodeURIComponent(key);
      value = encodeURIComponent(value);

      var kvp = search.substr(1).split('&');
      var i = 0;

      for(; i<kvp.length; i++){
        if (kvp[i].indexOf(key + '=') === 0) {
          var pair = kvp[i].split('=');
          pair[1] = value;
          kvp[i] = pair.join('=');
          break;
        }
      }

      if(i >= kvp.length){
        kvp[kvp.length] = [key,value].join('=');
      }

      var params = kvp.join('&');
      if(params.indexOf('&') === 0) {
        params = params.substr(1);
      }

      return '?' + params;
    }

<div class="lia-message-subject lia-component-message-view-widget-subject">
<div class="MessageSubject">
<div class="MessageSubjectIcons">
<a class="lia-link-navigation verified-icon" href="/t5/civil-3d-forum/dynamic-block-strech-and-rotate-actions-not-cooperating/m-p/12787484#M513304" id="link_8"><span alt="Solved!" aria-label="Solved!" class="lia-img-message-type-solved lia-fa-message lia-fa-type lia-fa-solved lia-fa" id="display_1" role="img" title="Solved!"></span></a>
<h2 class="message-subject" itemprop="name">
<span class="lia-message-unread">
<div class="lia-message-subject">
							Dynamic Block Strech and Rotate Actions Not Cooperating
						</div>
</span>
</h2>
<span alt="Message contains an attachment" aria-label="Contains an attachment" class="lia-img-message-has-attachment lia-fa-message lia-fa-has lia-fa-attachment lia-fa" id="display_5" role="img" title="Contains an attachment"></span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="lia-message-body lia-component-message-view-widget-body lia-component-body-signature-highlight-escalation lia-component-message-view-widget-body-signature-highlight-escalation" id="bodyDisplay" itemprop="text">
<div class="lia-message-body-content">
<p>I'm trying to create a block with simple stretch and rotation actions. I have this working almost 100%, but I'd really like to have the rotation grip stay fixed to the tip of the arrow after the base polyline is stretched. I've tried including the rotation action in the action set for the stretch, but then I end up with unexpected results when rotating the block after it's stretched. </p><p> </p><p>Does anyone have ideas on how I could adjust this to get the desired result?</p>
<div>
<div class="lia-panel-feedback-banner-safe">
<p>
					
						Solved!
					
					<a class="lia-link-navigation accepted-solution-link" href="/t5/civil-3d-forum/dynamic-block-strech-and-rotate-actions-not-cooperating/m-p/12787606#M513308" id="link_9">Go to Solution.</a>
</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="lia-message-subject lia-component-message-view-widget-subject">
<div class="MessageSubject">
<div class="MessageSubjectIcons">
<a class="lia-link-navigation verified-icon" href="/t5/civil-3d-forum/dynamic-block-strech-and-rotate-actions-not-cooperating/m-p/12787606#M513308" id="link_19"><span alt="Solution" aria-label="Solution" class="lia-img-message-type-solution lia-fa-message lia-fa-type lia-fa-solution lia-fa" id="display_6" role="img" title="Solution"></span></a>
<h2 class="message-subject">
<span class="lia-message-unread">
</span>
</h2>
<span alt="Message contains an image" aria-label="Contains an image" class="lia-img-message-has-image lia-fa-message lia-fa-has lia-fa-image lia-fa" id="display_7" role="img" title="Contains an image"></span>
<span alt="Message contains an attachment" aria-label="Contains an attachment" class="lia-img-message-has-attachment lia-fa-message lia-fa-has lia-fa-attachment lia-fa" id="display_5_0" role="img" title="Contains an attachment"></span>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="lia-message-body lia-component-message-view-widget-body lia-component-body-signature-highlight-escalation lia-component-message-view-widget-body-signature-highlight-escalation" id="bodyDisplay_0" itemprop="text">
<div class="lia-message-body-content">
<div class="lia-message-body-accepted-solution-checkmark"></div>
<p>You can do this with a more simplistic approach.  Replace the linear parameter and rotation parameter with a Polar Parameter and a Polar Stretch action.  It can to both stretching and rotation in one action.  Include the point/move for the attribute in the polar stretch action.  The point/move action will chain with the stretch and rotation of the polar stretch.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><span class="lia-inline-image-display-wrapper lia-image-align-inline" image-alt="MMcCall402_0-1716303147936.png" style="width: 600px;"><img alt="MMcCall402_0-1716303147936.png" class="lia-media-image" li-bindable="" li-bypass-lightbox-when-linked="true" li-image-display-id="'1365237i63CBA123BEE2BCB7'" li-image-url="https://forums.autodesk.com/t5/image/serverpage/image-id/1365237i63CBA123BEE2BCB7?v=v2" li-message-uid="'12787606'" li-messages-message-image="true" li-use-hover-links="false" role="button" src="https://forums.autodesk.com/t5/image/serverpage/image-id/1365237i63CBA123BEE2BCB7/image-size/medium?v=v2&amp;px=400" tabindex="0" title="MMcCall402_0-1716303147936.png"/></span></p>
<p> </p>
<div class="UserSignature lia-message-signature">
<p><strong>Mark Mccall </strong><br/>CAD Mangler</p><br/><p><img height="27" src="https://i.ibb.co/wrnrQ2m/autodesk-expert-elite-logo-1line-rgb-black.png" width="251"/></p><br/><p style="font-size:18px"><strong><span style="color:#005780">Hammer Land Engineering</span></strong></p><br/><p style="font-size:18px"><a href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/mark-mccall-bb274722/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer"><span style="color:#3366ff">Linked</span><span style="background-color:#3366ff;color:#ffffff">in</span></a></p>
